10a5(myang 'das): tu gzhag nas/ phyogs gcig tu cang mi smra bar 'khod de// de'i tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA gsum gyi bye ma snyed kyi dge bsnyen ma khrims lnga yongasu srung ba spyod lam dang
10a6(myang 'das): ldan pa la 'di lta ste/ dge bsnyen ma 'tshe ba'i yon tan dang / dge bsnyen ma dpal gyi 'phreng ba dang / dge bsnyen ma phyi ba'i zer sha ka la sogs pas thog mar drangs nas/ ngage bstan pa
10a7(myang 'das): brgyad khri bzhi stong snyed thams cad kyang / dam pa'i chos yongasu 'dzin pa/ sems can tshad med pa brgya stong gdul ba'i phyir/ bud med kyi lusu ston cing / khyim gyi chos yongasu spong
10a8(myang 'das): pa bdag gi lus la sbrul gdug pa bzhi dang 'dra bar rtogs pa/ lus la rtag tu srin bu grangs med ba za ba dang / lus 'di la shin tu btsug pa dang / 'dod pas yongasu bcings pan
10b1(myang 'das): rdzogs ga/ lus 'di la khyi ro dang 'dra bar 'jig su rung ba dang / lus 'di ni mi gtsang ba ste/ bug dgu nas rtag tu zag par rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni mkhar dang 'dra ste/ sha dang lpags pa
10b2(myang 'das): dang / rtswa dang / rgyas pas rnam par dkris pa/ lag pa dang rkang pa ni mkhar gyi nyen lta bur gyur pa/ mig ni skar khung lta bur gyur pa/ mgo bo ni khang pa lta bur gyur te/ sems rgyal po
10b3(myang 'das): dang 'dra ba/ de'i nang na gnas par rtogs pa/ lus 'khar dang 'dra ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongasu spangs te/ bus pa so so'i skye bo dag ni dri la rags par
10b4(myang 'das): byed do// 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug gi srin po ga nas par rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni snying po med pa ste/ 'dam bu'i myu gu 'am/ e ran 'da' 'am/ chu'i chu bur ram/ 
10b5(myang 'das): chu shing lta bur rtogs pas/ lus 'di ni mi rtag pa ste/ skad ci ga skad cig tu 'pho zhing / dper na glog gi 'od ngam/ ga zar de'i chu'am/ sgyu ma 'am/ smig sgyu 'am/ 
10b6(myang 'das): tshul ri mor bris pa lta bur rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni 'gyur zhing 'pho ba ste/ dper na chu 'gram g.yang sa'i sdong po lta bur rtogs pa/ lus 'di ni ring por mi thogs pa ste/ sbyang ki dang / 
10b7(myang 'das): phar ba dang / srin bya dang / 'ug pa dang / brgod dang / khwa dang / sgeg dang / khyi ltogs pa'i zan du gyur te/ 'di la mkhas pa shes can su zhig mos shing chags par byad snyam
10b8(myang 'das): du rtogs pa/ bi rlig gi nang du rgya mtsho chen po'i chu blugs kyang bzod kyi/ lus 'di mi rtag pa dang / mi gtsang ba dang / brtsog pa ni brjod sla ba ma yin par rtogs pa/ sa chen po
11a1(myang 'das): 'di rgya shug tsam du dril tam/ chung ngu na yungs kar gyi 'bru 'am/ rdul phra mor gse ba ni sla'i// lus 'di'i nyes pa'i skyon brjod pa ni slab ma yin par rtogs pa/ 
11a2(myang 'das): de bas na mchil ma dang 'dra bar yongasu spangs nas/ de'i rgyu de'i rkyen gyis/ dge bsnyen ma rnams stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon po med pa'i chos la rtag tu nan tan byed pa/ 
11a3(myang 'das): theg pa chen po'i mdo sde nyan cing 'dzin pa la mos pa/ thos nas kyang gzhan la rgya cher ston nus pa/ sngon gyi smon lam yongasu 'dzin pa/ bud med kyi lus la shin tu smod pa/ shin tu
11a4(myang 'das): skyon che bar shes pa/ snying po med par rtogs pa/ sems rtag tu rnal 'byor du spyod pa/ de bzhin du yang dag par rtogs cing mtha' med par 'khor ba'i rgyun yongasu gcod pa/ 
11a5(myang 'das): theg pa chen po la skom pas gdungs pa ltar mos pa/ bdag shin tu ngoms pas/ gzhan yang shin tu ngoms par byed pa/ theg pa chen po la rab tu mos pa/ theg pa chen
11a6(myang 'das): po shin tu srung ba/ bud med kyi lus su ston kyang yang dag par byang chub sems dpa' sha stag ste/ thams cad kyang 'jig rten gyi bsam pa dang / shin tu sbyor ba/ ma
11a7(myang 'das): rgal ba sgrol ba/ ma grol ba 'grol ba/ dkon mchog gsum gyi gdung rgyun mi 'chad pa 'tshob pa/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su chos kyi 'khor lo skor bar 'gyur ba/ rgyan chen pos
11a8(myang 'das): yong su brgyan pa/ tshul khrims yongasu srung ba/ de lta bu'i yon tan tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la snying rje'i sems bskyed cing / bu gcig dang 'dra bar gnyis
11b1(myang 'das): med par mnyam pa sha stago/ de dag kyang snga dro'i dus nyi ma thog ma shar ba na/ 'od kyis reg nas gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ dang ni shing sa la drung gnyis kyi drung du 'deng ngo // zhes
11b2(myang 'das): smraso// ngag bsnyen ma rnams kyis mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa/ snga ma bas phyed kyis bzang bar sbyar te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi
11b3(myang 'das): nges phyag 'tshal te/ lan brgya stong bskor nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis/ sangs rgyas dang dge 'dun du bcas pa la/ mchod
11b4(myang 'das): pa'i yo byad bshams pa 'di/ de bzhin gsheg/ sa pas thugs brtse ba'i slad du bzhes shig ces gsol to// de la bcom ldan 'das cang mi gsung bar bzhi su ma
11b5(myang 'das): gnong// dge bsnyen ma rnams bsams pa bzhin ma gyur pas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA bzhi'i bye ma snyed kyi
11b6(myang 'das): tsa byi'i bu/ grong khyer yangs pa can na gnas pa'i skyes pa dang / bud med dang / khye'u dang / bu mau dang / chung ma dang / 'khor rnams dang / gzhan yang 'dzam+bu'i gling gi rgyal
11b7(myang 'das): rig su gtogs pa/ rgyal po'i 'khor dang bcas te thams cad kyang / chos 'dod pa'i phyir/ tshul khrims yongasu srung ba/ spyod lam dang ldan pa/ slob pa gzhan la zhugs shi
11b8(myang 'das): dam pa'i chos la sun 'byin pa shin tu tshar gcod pa sha stag gcig la gcig 'di skad ces dam 'cha'o// bdag cag gser dang dngul dang / rin po che'i gter mdzong lta
12a1(myang 'das): bur/ yang dag pa'i chos shin tu zab mo bdud rtsi lta bu zad mi shes pa/ yun tu 'jig rten na gnas par byas te/ bdag cag kyang de dag la rtag tu nan tan spyod par
12a2(myang 'das): gyur cig/ gal te zhal nas gsungs pa'i dam pa'i chos la/ dbang za zhing skur pa zhig yod na/ bdag cag gis de'i lce gcad do zhes dam bcas shing / gzhan yang khyim nas/ 
12a3(myang 'das): khyim ma yin par rab tu byung ba dag/ tshul khrims las nyams par gyur na/ bdag cag gis khyim par phab ste/ las byed du gzhu go zhes pa dang / gal te dam pa'i chos la nan tan du
12a4(myang 'das): byed na/ bdag cag gis pha ma dang 'dra bar/ rim gro dang / bkur sti bya'o zhes pa dang / gal te dge 'dun las dam pa'i chos la nan tan du spyod pa zhig yod na/ bdag cag
12a5(myang 'das): gis rje su yi rang zhing de la mthu yang sbyin par bya'o zhes/ dam bcas pa/ rtag tu theg pa chen po'i mdo sde thos pa/ mos shing / thos nas kyang gzhan la rgyas par ston pa de
12a6(myang 'das): lta bu'i yon tan dang ldan pa sha stag la 'di lta ste/ li tsa byi'i bu rnam dag dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / li tsa ti'i bu bag yod pa rnam par dag pa dang / li tsa byi'i bu rtag tu dri med rnam
12a7(myang 'das): ngag yon tan la sogs te/ de dag gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ kye grogs po dag myur bar de bzhin gau shegs pa gang na ba der song ste/ mchod pa phun sum tshogs pa rnam pa
12a8(myang 'das): sna tshogs kyis mchod du 'ding ngo // de nas li tsa byi de dag re res kyang / bal glang brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / rin po che'i shing rta/ rta bzhi la bcas pa brgyad khri bzhi stong dang / yid
12b1(myang 'das): bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che brgyad khri ba'i stong dang / gzhan yang shing tsan dan dang / a ga ru sbams pa brgyad khri bzhi stong snyed pa shams te/ bal glang de re re'i mdun na rin po che'i rgyal
12b2(myang 'das): mtshan dang / ba dan dang / gdugs kyang ba sham so// gdugs nang gi chu ru yang kho ra khor yug tu dpag tshad gcig khab so// ba dan nang gi chu ngu yang ring khyang dpag tshad sum cu rtsa gnyis// 
12b3(myang 'das): rin po che'i rgyal mtshan nang gi chu ngu yang mtho khyad dpag tshad brgya pa ste/ de lta bu'i mchod pa'i yo byad bshams nas/ sangs rgyas gang na par lhags te/ phyin pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi
12b4(myang 'das): zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis sangs rgyas dang / dge slong gi
12b5(myang 'das): dge 'dun rnams la// mchod pa'i yo byad 'di dag dbul na/ de bzhin gshegs pas bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ mchod pa 'di dag bzhes shig ces gsol to// 
12b6(myang 'das): de la de bzhin gshegs bcang mi gsung nas ban sum gnang // li tsa byi'i bu rnams bsams pa bzhin ma gyur nas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis non te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyi rlab
12b7(myang 'das): kyis/ sa las shing ta la bdun srid tsam du 'phags nas/ steng gi na mkha' la cang mi smra bar 'khod do// de'o tshe gzhan yang klung gang+gA lnga'i bye ma snyed kyi blon po chen po dang / khyim bdag
12b8(myang 'das): dang / tshong dpon thag pa chen po la shin tu mos pas/ slob pa gzhan la zhugs pa gang zhig yang dag pa'i chos la smod pa zhig yod na/ de dag gi mthus thul pa ni/ ji ltar rtsa ba dang / 
13a1(myang 'das): // shing la ser ba bab pa lta bu sha stag la 'di lta ste/ tshong dpon nyi ma'i 'od dang / tshong dpon 'jig rten skyong dang / tshong dpon chos skyong la sogs pas thog mar
13a2(myang 'das): drangs te/ de dag gis so nas mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa ni/ snga ma bas lnga 'gyur tsam bshams te/ shing sa la drung gnyis kyi bar gang na ba der song ste/ phyin pa dang / bcom ldan
13a3(myang 'das): 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ lan brgya stong du bskor te/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis/ sangs rgyas dang dge
13a4(myang 'das): slong gi dge 'dun rnams la/ mchod pa'i yo byad 'di dag 'bul na/ bzhes shig ces gsol to// de la de bzhin gshegs pas cang mi gsungs nas gzhesu ma gan // tshong dpon
13a5(myang 'das): de dag bsams pa bzhin ma gyur nas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis// yid gdungs par gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis byin gyis rlabs kyis/ sa las shing ta la bdun srid du
13a6(myang 'das): 'phags nas/ steng gi na mkha' la cang mi smra bar 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang yul yangs pa can gyi rgyal po/ btsun mo dang / sras su bcas/ gzhan yang 'dzam+bu gling na rgyal po
13a7(myang 'das): ma skyes dgra ma gtogs par/ rgyal phran de ma yin pa thams cad dang / grong khyer dang / ljongs dang / grong 'dab thams cad kyi mi thams cad dang bcas pa la/ 'di lta ste/ rgyal po
13a8(myang 'das): zla 'od dri med rgyal po la sogs pas thog mar drangs nas/ so so nas dmag rnam bzhi dang bcas te/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhag so// rgyal po de dag re re yang 'khor khri phrag brgyad
13b1(myang 'das): cu dang bca so// dmag gi tshogs kyang bal glang dang / rta pa ste/ bal glang de dag kyang mche ba drug dang ldan la/ rta rnams kyang mgyogs khyad rlung bzhin te/ mchod pa'i yo byad bshams pa
13b2(myang 'das): yang snga ma bas drug 'gyur gyis lha go// rin po che'i gdugs nang gi chu ngu yang / chu zheng kho ra khor yug tu dpag tshad brgyad khebaso// ba dan nang gi thung ngu yang ring khad dpag tshad bcu
13b3(myang 'das): drug snyed do// rin po che'i rgyal mtshan nang gi chung ngu yang mtho khyad dpag tshad sum cu rtsa drug/ rgyal po de dag thams cad kyang / yang dag pa'i chos la gnas pas/ log pa'i chos kun
13b4(myang 'das): la shin tu smod pa/ theg pa chen po la bkur sti byung pa/ theg po chen po la shin tu mas pa/ sems can thams cad bu cig/ dang 'dra bar byams pa/ zhal zas pa shams
13b5(myang 'das): ba'i dri yang dpag tshad bzhi'i bar du bre ba bshams nas/ snga dro'i dus kyi tshe mchod pa'i yo byad rnam pa sna tshogs thogs te/ shing sa la drung gnyis kyi bar de bzhin ga bye
13b6(myang 'das): ba gang na bzhugs pa der song nas phyin pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag gis/ sangs rgyas dang / dge slong gi dge 'dun rnams
13b7(myang 'das): la mchod pa'ang dag 'bul na/ de bzhin gshegs pas thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ bdag cag gi mchod pa tha ma 'di bzhes shig ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa dus mkhyen
13b8(myang 'das): bas bzhes su ma gnang ngo // rgyal po de dag kyang bsams pa bzhin du ma gyur pas/ shin tu mya ngan gyis yid gdungs par gyur te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe gzhan yang klung
14a1(myang 'das): / gan bdun gyi byer snyed kyi rgyal po'i btsun po rnams tshogs te/ de la gcig ma gtogs pa ni/ ma skyes dgra'i btsun mo 'ba' shig// sems can gradu pa'i byi
14a2(myang 'das): bud med kyi lusu ston te/ rtag tu lus kyis nan tan du spyod cing / stong pa nyid dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / smon pa med pa'i chos la sems 'dris shing goms par byed pa de la sogaso te/ 
14a3(myang 'das): btsun mo khams gsum bzang mo dang / btsun mo 'dod pa'i yon tan la sogs pas thog drang so// thams cad kyang dam pa'i chos la gnas shing / tshul khrims yongasu srung ba/ spyod
14a4(myang 'das): lam dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cad la bu gcig pa dang 'dra bar nyams pa sha stag go// de dag kyang gcig la gcig 'di skad du/ bdag cag kyang myur bar
14a5(myang 'das): sangs rgyas gang na bzhugs par 'dong ngo zhes smraso// rgyal po'i btsun mo rnams kyis mchod pa'i yo byad ba mas pa ni/ snga ma pas bdun 'gyur gyis lhag ste/ matog
14a6(myang 'das): dang / spos dang / rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / dar gyi ba dan dang / gdugs dang / zhal zas mchog rnamaso// rin po che'i gdugs nang gi mu ru yang / chu zheng kho ra khor yug tu
14a7(myang 'das): dpag tshad bcu drug khebs so// ba dan nang gi chung ngu'i tshad kyang dpag tshad sum cu cu drug skyed ngo // rin po che'i rgyal mtshan nang gi dma' bo'i ched kyang dpag tshad drug cu rtsa brgyad
14a8(myang 'das): snyed do// zhal zas kyi dri bsung gis kyang dpag tshad brgyad kyi bar du brog mchod pa'i yo bad de lta bu dag bshams nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa ga la ba der song ste phyin pa dang / bcom
20b1(myang 'das): bas cang mi gsung bar bzhesu ma gnang // de nas lha rnams kyang bsams pa bzhin du ma gyur pas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdungs te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de la gcig
20b2(myang 'das): ma gtogs pa ni srid pa'i rtse mo ste/ tshangs pa'i ris kyi lha rnams kyang 'dus par gyur to// de'i tshe tshangs pa'i rgyal po dang / tshangs ris kyi lha rnams kyi 'od kyis/ gling bzhi
20b3(myang 'das): kun snang bar byas nas/ 'dod pa'i khams na/ lha dang mi dang / nyi zla'i 'od kyang mi snang bar byas so// de dag kyang so so nas rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / bdar dang / gdug
20b4(myang 'das): thogs pa ni/ ba dan nang gi thung ngu yang tshangs pa'i gnam nas shing sa la'i tshal la thug pa thogs nas/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags te/ bcom ldan 'das
20b5(myang 'das): kyi zhabs la spyi bos pag 'tshal nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ bdag
20b6(myang 'das): cag gi mchod pa nang gi tha ma 'di bzhes shig ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa dus mkhyen pas cang mi gsung bas bzhisum gan // tshangs pa'i lha rnams bsams
20b7(myang 'das): pa bzhin du ma gyur nas/ mya ngan gyis yid gdudus te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// de'i tshe lha ma yin gyi rgyal po thag zangs rigs kyang lha ma yin gyi 'khor dpag tu med
20b8(myang 'das): ba dang btsas te lhag so// de rnams kyi lus kyi 'od kyang tshangs pa'i lha bas lhag par gyur te/ rin po che'i rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / gdugs rnams thogs te/ gdag
21a1(myang 'das): / nang gi chung ngu yang stong chung ngu'i 'jig rten gyi khams khebs pa dang / phul byung ba'i zhal zas mchog rnams thogs nas/ sangs rgyas gang ra bar lhags
21a2(myang 'das): te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bas phyag 'tshal nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das bdag cag la thugs brje ba'i slad du/

21a8(myang 'das): du 'gyur ba/ me rab tu 'bar ba yang bsil ba'i char gyis zhi bar byas nas/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis rlabs kyis/ bdud kyi 'khor rnams kyang 'di snyam du sems bskyed par
21b1(myang 'das): gyur to// thams cad kyis ral gri dang / mda' gzhu dang / go tsa dang / mtshon shag ti dang / lcags kyu dang / lcags tho dang / dgra sta dang / 'khor lo dang / zhags pa la sogs
21b2(myang 'das): te/ mtshon cha thams cad spangs nas/ mchod pa'i yo byad lha dang mi las khyad par du gyur pa bsham so// gdugs nang gi chung ngu yang stong 'bring po'i 'jig rten gyi khams
21b3(myang 'das): khebs pa thogs nas/ sangs rgyas gang na bar lhags te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la spyi bos phyag 'tshal nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// 
21b4(myang 'das): bcom ldan 'das bdag cag kyang theg pa chen po la rab tu dad cing mos te/ theg pa chen po bsrung b.ro 'tshal lo// bcom ldan 'das rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo gang
21b5(myang 'das): zhig khe dang / grags pa'i phyir ram/ ga zhan yang skrag par bya ba'i phyir ram/ gzhan la brdzun bya ba'i phyir ram/ nor dang / zang zing gi phyir ram/ gzhan gyi yid dang
21b6(myang 'das): sbyor ba tsam gyi pir/ theg po chen po 'di' dzin par byed na/ bden yong rung brdzun yang rung / bdag gi sa de'i tshe gang zag de'i 'jigs pa gsal ba'i pir/

21b8(myang 'das): chos smra ba dang / yang dag pa'i chos kyi bar du mi gcod pa dang / mu stegs can gdul ba dang / bdag gi lus bsrung ba dang / yang dag pa'i chos srung ba dang / theg pa chen
22a1(myang 'das): bsrung ba'i slad du gsang sngags 'di 'bu'o// gang gis gsang sngags 'di yid la bgyid na/ bal glang rmigs pas 'jigs pa dang bral bar 'gyur/ gal
22a2(myang 'das): te 'brog dgon pa 'am/ yul sa stong pa bag tsha ba'i gan su mchis na yang 'jigs par mi 'gyur/ chu dang / me dang / seng ge dang / stag dang / spyang ki dang / dgras 'jig
22a3(myang 'das): pa dang / rgyal po'i chad pas 'jigs pa las yang thar par 'gyu ro// bcom ldan 'das gang gis gsang sngags 'di yid la bgyid na/ 'jigs pa de dag la sogs pa thams cad
22a4(myang 'das): dang bral bar 'gyur ro// bcom ldan 'das gsang sngags 'di 'dzin pa la/ bdag cag gis bskyabs cing sba ba ni/ ji ltar ru sAl yan lag drug sbed ba bzhi no// bcom ldan 'das
22a5(myang 'das): bdag cag ni g.yo dang skyes 'di skad du smra ba ma la gas kyi/ gang gzungs sngags 'di 'dzin pa la/ bdag cag gis mthu stobs bsto // bcom ldan 'das bdag cag
22a6(myang 'das): la thugs brtse ba'i slad du/ mchod pa tha ma 'di bzhe su gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis bdud sdig to can la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// khyed kyis mchod pa zhal zasu

94a3(myang 'das): gshegs pa yang de dang 'dra ste/ nyon mongs pa zad da med kyang / chos kyi sku ni rtag tu yod do// rigs kyi bu de khyod kyi yid la ji snyam snang ba dang / me mar gyi snod cig char
94a4(myang 'das): med par 'gyur ram/ 'od srung gis gsol ba ma lag so// bcom ldan 'das cig car ma mchis pa ma lags kyang mi rtag par 'dra'o// ci ste chos kyi sku mar gyi snod dang

94b1(myang 'das): bas me mar zang ba lta bu zhes byar mi rung // de bas na ngas sngon mtshan ma dgag pa'i phyir me mar zad pa lta bu zhes bshad kyi/ yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa chen po ni me mar zang

94b4(myang 'das): yod pas phyir ldog pa zhes pa/ song ba dang ldog pa med pas phyir mi ldog pa zhes bya'o// // 'phags pa yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i mang//

94b8(myang 'das): na/ shing gi mi de ni kun gyis mthong bar rung gi/ brkyang ba dang / bskum pa dang / dgye ba dang / dgu pa ni ning nas bsgyur bar ma 'tshal te// sangs rgyas kyi ches

202'a3(myang 'das): sti byed pa ni/ ji ltar rgyal po chen pos sman pa mkhas pa la bkur sti byed pa bzhin no// ji ltar sman pa mkhas pas nges par 'chi bar 'gyur pa mi gso ba bzhin du/ mya ngan las
202'a4(myang 'das): 'das pa chen po'i mdo sde 'di yang de dang 'dra ste/ lo/ ga sred can la gso bar mi 'gyuraro// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang 'di lta ste dper na/ sman pa mkhas pa rig
202'a5(myang 'das): ba'i gnas brgyad la mkhas pa dag nad thams cad gso nus kyang nges par 'chi bar 'gyur ba'i nad gso nus pan ma yin no// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams
202'a6(myang 'das): kyang de dang radra ste/ sems can gyi srid pa kha na ma tho ba thams cad gso nus kyang nges par 'chi bar 'gyur ba lta bu log sred can dag gso nus pa ni ma yin no// rigs kyi bu gany+dza
202'a7(myang 'das): yang 'di lta ste dper na/ sman pa mkhas pa rig pa'i gnas brgyad la mkhas pa/ sman dbang kun dang rig po'i gnas brgyad kyi pha rol tu phyin te/ thams cad rtogs nas sngar bu la
202'a8(myang 'das): chu'i nang nas 'thung ba dang / skams las 'thung ba dang / ri las 'thung ba'i sman thams cad ston to// de dag shes nas 'gas kyis rig pa'i gnas brgyad kyang ston to// de nas
202'b1(myang 'das): ma yin pa dpyad gsang ba'i mchog kyang ston to// de bzhin gshegs pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang de dang 'dra ste/ sngar sras dang 'dra ba'i dge slong rnams la nyon
202'b2(myang 'das): mongs pa thams cad bsal ba'i thabs bstan te/ lus gtsang bar bya ba'i snying po med pa'i 'du shes la nan tan byed du bcug pa de ni/ chu dang / skams dang / ri brags lta bu bsdam
202'b3(myang 'das): pa'o// chu zhes bya ba ni lus sdug bsngal myong ba/ chu'i chu bur dang 'dra'o zhes bstan pa'o// skams zhes bya ba ni lus 'di snying po med de/ chu shing dang 'dra'o// zhes bstan pa'o// 
202'b4(myang 'das): ri brags zhes bya ba ni nyon mongs pa'i nang na bdag med po'i 'du shes bsgom pa bstan pa ste/ de bas na lus la bdag med pa zhes bya'o// de bzhin gshegs pas de ltar nye
202'b5(myang 'das): gnas rnams la bags kyis mdo sde dgu pa bstan te/ rtogs par byas nas de'i 'og tu de bzhin ga/ shegs pa'i snying po bstan te/ sras lta bu'i phyir/ de'i zhan
202'b6(myang 'das): gshegs pas rta go zhes pa bshad do// de bzhin gshegs pas de ltar theg pa chen po'i mdo sde mya ngan las 'das pa bstan pa ni/ sems can gang sems skyed dam/

202'b8(myang 'das): tshad med mtha' yas pa ste/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// de bas na 'di ni sman mkhas pa'i mchog phul du gyur pa/ gtso bor gyur pa/ mdo sde kun gyi rgyal ba lta bu'o// rigs
203a1(myang 'das): kyi bu gzhan yang 'di lta ste dper na/ gru chen po ni rgya mtsho'i tshu rol nas/ rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu sgrol la/ rgya mtsho'i pha rol nas tshu rol tu yang sgrol lo// de bzhin

203a3(myang 'das): gang du 'gro bar 'gyur ba yod na/ de dang de dag tu sgrol zhing de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mthong bar mdzad do// de bzhin de bzhin gshegs pa ni gru sgrol ba'i mkhan po lta bu'o//

208a6(myang 'das): ni/ skyes bu'i mtshan dang ldan pa zhes ngas poshad do// de la bud med gang zhig gal te bdag la sangs rgyas kyi rang bzhin yod par shes na/ de ni skyes pa zhes bya'o// rigs kyi bu
208a7(myang 'das): theg pa chen po yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa'i mdo sde 'di ni tshad med dpag tu med/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i bsod nams kyi phung por rig par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de bzhin
208a8(myang 'das): gshegs pa'i gsang pa'i snying po 'chad pa'i phyir ro// de bas na rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo dag/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang pa'i snying po myur du shes par 'dod na/ 
208b1(myang 'das): mdo sde 'di la sbyor ba'i nan tan brtson 'grusu bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' 'od srung gis/ bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/ de de bzhi no// de de bzhino// bcom ldan 'das kyis bka'
208b2(myang 'das): stsal pa bzhin te/ bdag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsang ba'i snying po rtogs pas/ skyes bu'i mtshan dang ldano// de bzhin gshegs pas bskul bas nges par rtogs par

208b4(myang 'das): chos kyi rjesu 'jug pa ma lag so// bcom ldan 'das kyis 'od srung la bka' stsal pa/ legaso shin tu leg so// khyod kyi shes pa ni bla na med pa'i chos kyi ro shin tu zab mo
208b5(myang 'das): shes par dka' ba shes te/ ji ltar bung ba dag kha dog la mi gnod pa ra ro myong ba bzhi no// rigs kyi bu gzhan yang 'di lta ste/ dper na/ sgra bu'i gcin gyis sa chen
208b6(myang 'das): po 'di brlan par mi nuso// ma 'ongs pa'i dus su mdo sde 'di 'phel ba yang de dang 'dra ste/ dam pa'i chos rnam par 'jig du nye ba na/ mdo sde phyogs 'dir sngar nub par 'gyur ro//

208b8(myang 'das): par char pa 'bab bo// theg pa chen po yongasu mya ngan las 'das pa'i mdo sde 'di yang de dang 'dra ste/ lho phyogs kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi phyir/ shin tu rgyas par 'gyur
